## Analysis

The Ground Truth (GT) is:
$$f(t, A) = -0.15728 \cdot A + 0.49114 \cdot \sin(\log(A + 1))$$

Note that the GT has `_t = 3.12275` multiplied by `c1 = 0.15728`, giving `0.49114` as the coefficient of the sin term. The variable `t` does not actually appear as a free variable â€” it's absorbed into the constant. So the GT is effectively a function of A only:

$$f(A) = -0.15728 \cdot A + 0.49114 \cdot \sin(\log(A + 1))$$

**Candidate 3**: `A*c0 + c1 + c2*sin(c3*log(A*c4 + 1) + c5)`

Setting:
- `c0 = -0.15728` (coefficient of A)
- `c1 = 0` (no constant offset in GT)
- `c2 = 0.49114` (coefficient of sin)
- `c3 = 1` (coefficient inside log)
- `c4 = 1` (so `A*c4 + 1 = A + 1`)
- `c5 = 0` (no phase shift)

This gives: `-0.15728*A + 0 + 0.49114*sin(1*log(A*1 + 1) + 0) = -0.15728*A + 0.49114*sin(log(A + 1))`

This exactly matches the GT.

Several other candidates also match (e.g., candidates 2, 4, 5, 9, 10, 12, 17, 24, 35, etc.) by setting their extra terms' coefficients to zero, but **Candidate 3** is the simplest and most direct match.
